        FROM mfo_permisoplan p
        INNER JOIN mfo_accionsist a ON a.id_accionSist = p.id_accionSist

        WHERE a.estado = 1

        FROM mfo_permisoplan p
        INNER JOIN mfo_accionsist a ON a.id_accionSist = p.id_accionSist
